Design System/Examples/Icons

design-system-examples-icons--docs · ./stories/examples/Icons.mdx
import {
  Meta,
  Unstyled,
  Source,
} from '@storybook/addon-docs/blocks';

<Meta title="Design System/Examples/Icons" />

## Icons

The `DIcon` component is a versatile icon component that can be configured to use different icon fonts. It supports both traditional icon fonts and material-style icon fonts.

### Configuration

The `DIcon` component is configured using the `DContextProvider`. The `DContextProvider` accepts an `icon` object with the following properties:

- `familyPrefix`: The prefix for the icon class (e.g., `bi-` for Bootstrap).
- `familyClass`: The class for the icon family (e.g., `bi-icon` for Bootstrap icons).
- `materialStyle`: A boolean flag that determines how the icon is rendered. If `true`, the icon is rendered with the name of the icon in the content of the tag. If `false`, the icon is rendered with the class of the icon font.

<Source
  code={`
<DContextProvider
  icon={{
    familyClass: 'bi',
    familyPrefix: 'bi-',
    materialStyle: false,
  }}
>
  <DIcon name="user" />
</DContextProvider>
  `}
  language="html"
/>


### Material Style Flag

This flag comes in handy when you have icon fonts that need to be included as the content of the tag.

Following example show the output of `DIcon` component with and without the `materialStyle` flag.

<Source
  code={`
  // Disabled Material Style Flag (default)
<i class="bi bi-user"></i>
  `}
  language="html"
/>

<Source
  code={`
  // Enabled Material Style Flag
<i class="bi">user</i>
  `}
  language="html"
/>


## Example Usage


#### Font Awesome Icons

To use Font Awesome icons, configure the `DContextProvider` as follows:

```jsx
<DContextProvider
  icon={{
    familyPrefix: 'fa-',
    familyClass: 'fa-solid',
    materialStyle: false,
  }}
>
  <DIcon name="user" />
</DContextProvider>
```

#### Material Icons

To use Material icons, configure the `DContextProvider` as follows:

```jsx
<DContextProvider
  icon={{
    familyPrefix: '',
    familyClass: 'material-symbols-outlined',
    materialStyle: true,
  }}
>
  <DIcon name="user" />
</DContextProvider>
```

Design System/Foundations/Color Tokens

design-system-foundations-color-tokens--docs · ./stories/foundations/ColorTokens.mdx
import { Meta } from '@storybook/addon-docs/blocks';

# Color Tokens

Dynamic Framework provides semantic color tokens with extended shades (25, 50, 100 … 900) for text, backgrounds, borders, badges, and buttons. Tokens: Primary, Success, Warning, Danger, Info, Secondary, Light, Dark. Light variants are designed for dark backgrounds.

<br />

### Text colors
Use text tokens to communicate state and semantics.

<div className="d-flex flex-wrap gap-3 mb-4">
  <p className="m-0 text-primary">.text-primary</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-success">.text-success</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-warning">.text-warning</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-danger">.text-danger</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-info">.text-info</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-secondary">.text-secondary</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-dark">.text-dark</p>
</div>

<div className="mt-2 mb-4">
  <p className="mb-1 small">Light variant (for dark backgrounds)</p>
  <div className="p-4 rounded" style={{ background: 'var(--bs-primary-800, #1a237e)' }}>
    <span className="text-light">.text-light (use on dark bg)</span>
  </div>
</div>

```html
<p class="text-success">Success text</p>
<p class="text-danger">Error text</p>
```

<br />

### Background tints (shades 25–900)
Apply subtle state backgrounds with shade suffixes.

<div className="d-flex flex-wrap gap-3 mb-4">
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-primary-25">.bg-primary-25</div>
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-primary-100">.bg-primary-100</div>
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-primary-900 text-white">.bg-primary-900</div>
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-success-100">.bg-success-100</div>
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-warning-100">.bg-warning-100</div>
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-danger-100">.bg-danger-100</div>
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-info-100">.bg-info-100</div>
  <div className="p-3 rounded bg-secondary-100">.bg-secondary-100</div>
</div>

```html
<div class="bg-primary-25 p-3 rounded">.bg-primary-25</div>
<div class="bg-primary-100 p-3 rounded">.bg-primary-100</div>
<div class="bg-primary-900 p-3 rounded text-white">.bg-primary-900</div>
```

<br />

### Borders
Use border tokens to frame elements.

<div className="d-flex flex-wrap gap-3 mb-4">
  <div className="p-2 rounded border border-primary">.border-primary</div>
  <div className="p-2 rounded border border-success">.border-success</div>
  <div className="p-2 rounded border border-warning">.border-warning</div>
  <div className="p-2 rounded border border-danger">.border-danger</div>
  <div className="p-2 rounded border border-info">.border-info</div>
  <div className="p-2 rounded border border-secondary">.border-secondary</div>
</div>

```html
<div class="border border-danger">…</div>
```

<br />

### Badges
Badges support semantic color tokens via text-bg-*.

<div className="d-flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4">
  <span className="badge text-bg-primary">Primary</span>
  <span className="badge text-bg-success">Success</span>
  <span className="badge text-bg-warning">Warning</span>
  <span className="badge text-bg-danger">Danger</span>
  <span className="badge text-bg-info">Info</span>
  <span className="badge text-bg-secondary">Secondary</span>
  <span className="badge text-bg-dark">Dark</span>
</div>

<div className="mt-2 mb-4">
  <p className="mb-1 small">Light variant (for dark backgrounds)</p>
  <div className="p-4 rounded" style={{ background: 'var(--bs-primary-800, #1a237e)' }}>
    <span className="badge text-bg-light text-dark">Light</span>
  </div>
</div>

```html
<span class="badge text-bg-success">Success</span>
```

<br />

### Buttons
Buttons support solid and outline variants with tokens.

<div className="d-flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4">
  <button className="btn btn-primary">Primary</button>
  <button className="btn btn-success">Success</button>
  <button className="btn btn-warning">Warning</button>
  <button className="btn btn-danger">Danger</button>
  <button className="btn btn-info">Info</button>
  <button className="btn btn-secondary">Secondary</button>
  <button className="btn btn-dark">Dark</button>
</div>

<div className="mt-2 mb-4">
  <p className="mb-1 small">Light variant (for dark backgrounds)</p>
  <div className="p-4 rounded" style={{ background: 'var(--bs-primary-800, #1a237e)' }}>
    <button className="btn btn-light text-dark me-2">Light</button>
    <button className="btn btn-outline-light">Light Outline</button>
  </div>
</div>

<div className="d-flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2 mb-4">
  <button className="btn btn-outline-primary">Outline Primary</button>
  <button className="btn btn-outline-success">Outline Success</button>
  <button className="btn btn-outline-warning">Outline Warning</button>
  <button className="btn btn-outline-danger">Outline Danger</button>
  <button className="btn btn-outline-info">Outline Info</button>
  <button className="btn btn-outline-secondary">Outline Secondary</button>
  <button className="btn btn-outline-dark">Outline Dark</button>
</div>

```html
<button class="btn btn-info">Info</button>
<button class="btn btn-outline-danger">Danger</button>
```

<br />

### Alerts
Semantic alerts styled with color tokens.

<div className="d-flex flex-column gap-2 mb-4">
  <div className="alert alert-primary m-0" role="alert">Primary alert — informative message.</div>
  <div className="alert alert-success m-0" role="alert">Success alert — action completed.</div>
  <div className="alert alert-warning m-0" role="alert">Warning alert — proceed carefully.</div>
  <div className="alert alert-danger m-0" role="alert">Danger alert — something went wrong.</div>
  <div className="alert alert-info m-0" role="alert">Info alert — additional context.</div>
  <div className="alert alert-secondary m-0" role="alert">Secondary alert — neutral notice.</div>
  <div className="alert alert-dark m-0" role="alert">Dark alert — emphasis on dark tones.</div>
</div>

```html
<div class="alert alert-success" role="alert">Success alert</div>
```

<br />

### Overlays and opacity
Use overlay opacity with state tints.

<div className="p-3 rounded bg-primary-100 overlay-50">Overlay 50%</div>

```html
<div class="bg-primary-100 overlay-50">…</div>
```

<br />

### Dark mode and utilities
- Prefer .text-light over dark surfaces.
- Combine tokens with dark: for system/forced dark contexts.
See: <a href="/?path=/story/design-system-examples-dark-utilities">Design System/Examples/Dark Utilities</a> and <a href="/?path=/story/design-system-foundations-extended-utilities">Foundations/Extended Utilities</a>.

<br />

## Accessibility guidance
- Ensure WCAG AA contrast when pairing text and backgrounds.
- Use semantic tokens consistently for clear communication.

</div>

Design System/Foundations/CSS Distribution

design-system-foundations-css-distribution--docs · ./stories/foundations/CSSDistribution.mdx
import { Meta, Unstyled } from '@storybook/addon-docs/blocks';

import { DAlert } from '../../src/components';

<Meta title="Design System/Foundations/CSS Distribution" />

<div className="inline-story sb-unstyled" style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--bs-body-font-family)' }}>

# CSS Distribution & Customization

<Unstyled>
  <DAlert color="info">
    Starting from version 2.3.0, only `dynamic-ui.css` and `dynamic-ui.min.css` are distributed.
    The previous variants `dynamic-ui-root.css` and `dynamic-ui-non-root.css`
    have been removed to simplify upgrades and avoid desynchronization issues.
  </DAlert>
</Unstyled>

### How to Customize

1. **Include the main CSS:**
    ```html
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="/path/to/dynamic-ui.css" />
    ```
2. **Override variables:**
  Add your own stylesheet or snippet after the main CSS to override any design tokens or variables:
    ```css
    :root {
      --bs-primary: #ff0055;
      --bs-body-font-family: 'Montserrat', sans-serif;
      /* ...other overrides... */
    }
    ```
3. **Safe upgrades:**
  All default variables are included in the main bundle, so new tokens are available automatically and removed ones do not break the theme.

<br />
### Example: Custom Theme Snippet

```html
<link rel="stylesheet" href="/path/to/dynamic-ui.css" />
<style>
  :root {
    --bs-primary: #ff0055;
    --bs-body-font-family: 'Montserrat', sans-serif;
    --bs-body-bg: #f5f5f5;
    --bs-border-radius: 0.75rem;
  }
</style>
```

<br />
### Migration Guide

- If you previously used `dynamic-ui-root.css` or `dynamic-ui-non-root.css`, switch to `dynamic-ui.css` and apply your overrides as shown above.
- For advanced theming, refer to the [Design Tokens](?path=/docs/design-system-foundations-design-tokens--docs) page and [docs.modyo.com](https://docs.modyo.com/en/dynamic/).

<br />
### FAQ

**Q: What happens if there are two `:root` blocks?**
<br />A: The last one loaded wins for each variable, thanks to CSS cascade. You can safely override any token after loading the main CSS.

**Q: How do I keep my theme up to date?**
<br />A: Since all tokens are included in the main bundle, you only need to override what you want. New tokens are available automatically after upgrades.

**Q: Where can I find a list of available tokens?**
<br />A: See the [Design Tokens](?path=/docs/design-system-foundations-design-tokens--docs) page or Storybook for a visual reference.

<br />

</div>

Design System/Foundations/Design Tokens

design-system-foundations-design-tokens--docs · ./stories/foundations/DesignTokens.mdx
import { Meta } from '@storybook/addon-docs/blocks';

<Meta title="Design System/Foundations/Design Tokens" />

<div className="inline-story sb-unstyled" style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--bs-body-font-family)' }}>

# Design Tokens

Dynamic Framework builds on Bootstrap 5 and exposes a robust set of CSS variables and Sass tokens to craft brand themes. Prefer overriding CSS variables at runtime for theming, and use Sass variables for build-time defaults when shipping a custom bundle. Official documentation is available at https://docs.modyo.com.

<br />

## Principles
- Scope overrides: use `:root` for global themes, `[data-bs-theme="brand"]` or `body.brand` for app-specific, and `.dark` or `prefers-color-scheme` for dark mode.
- Change variables, not classes: utilities and components read from CSS variables; overriding variables updates the whole system consistently.
- Validate contrast: ensure WCAG AA for text/background, borders, and focus rings.

<br />

### Core variables (what to override)
These variables drive components and utilities; override them to theme typography, colors, spacing, borders, shadows, and dark mode consistently.

#### Typography
Key CSS variables:
- Family and body: `--bs-body-font-family`, `--bs-body-font-size`, `--bs-body-line-height`
- Heading sizes: `--bs-fs-1` … `--bs-fs-6`
- Display sizes: `--bs-fs-display-1` … `--bs-fs-display-6`
- Small text: `--bs-fs-small`; line-heights: `--bs-lh-sm`, `--bs-lh-base`, `--bs-lh-lg`
- Heading line-height: `--bs-heading-line-height`

Example:
```css
:root {
  --bs-body-font-family: "Jost", system-ui, sans-serif; /* or your brand font */
  --bs-body-font-size: 1rem; /* base body size */
  --bs-fs-1: 3rem; /* h1 */
  --bs-fs-2: 2.5rem;
  --bs-fs-3: 2rem;
  --bs-fs-4: 1.5rem;
  --bs-fs-5: 1.25rem;
  --bs-fs-6: 1rem;
  --bs-fs-small: .875rem; /* small text */
}
```

#### Typography variables (headings and display)
```css
:root {
  /* Headings and body sizes */
  --bs-fs-1: 3rem;
  --bs-fs-2: 2.5rem;
  --bs-fs-3: 2rem;
  --bs-fs-4: 1.5rem;
  --bs-fs-5: 1.25rem;
  --bs-fs-6: 1rem;
  --bs-fs-small: .875rem;
  --bs-heading-line-height: 1.2;

  /* Display sizes */
  --bs-fs-display-1: 6rem;
  --bs-fs-display-2: 5.5rem;
  --bs-fs-display-3: 5rem;
  --bs-fs-display-4: 4.5rem;
  --bs-fs-display-5: 4rem;
  --bs-fs-display-6: 3.5rem;
}
```

#### Usage examples
```html
<h1 class="h1">Heading 1 (.h1)</h1>
<h6 class="h6">Heading 6 (.h6)</h6>
<div class="display-1">Display 1</div>
<div class="display-6">Display 6</div>
<p class="fs-1 m-0">.fs-1</p>
<p class="fs-6 m-0">.fs-6</p>
<p class="small m-0">Small text (.small)</p>
```

<br />

#### Color system
Dynamic’s palettes expose base tokens and extended shades.
- Base semantic tokens: `--bs-primary`, `--bs-success`, `--bs-warning`, `--bs-danger`, `--bs-info`, `--bs-secondary`, `--bs-light`, `--bs-dark`
- Extended shades by state: e.g., `--bs-primary-25`, `--bs-primary-50`, …, `--bs-primary-900`
- Text/background/border subtles: `--bs/{token}-text-emphasis`, `--bs/{token}-bg-subtle`, `--bs/{token}-border-subtle`
- Body defaults: `--bs-body-color`, `--bs-body-bg`, links: `--bs-link-color`, `--bs-link-hover-color`

Override with either RGB bases or direct colors:
```css
:root {
  /* Brand primaries */
  --bs-primary: #0b74ff;
  --bs-primary-100: #e5f0ff; /* light tint */
  --bs-success: #0c8a50;
  --bs-warning: #d99100;
  --bs-danger: #c83333;
  --bs-info: #0aa0c8;
  --bs-secondary: #5b6670;

  /* Body and links */
  --bs-body-color: #2e3438;
  --bs-body-bg: #ffffff;
  --bs-link-color: #0b74ff;
  --bs-link-hover-color: #095fd1;
}
```

#### Palette variables (25–900)
```css
:root {
  /* Primary */
  --bs-primary-25: /* override */; --bs-primary-50: /* override */; --bs-primary-100: /* override */;
  --bs-primary-200: /* override */; --bs-primary-300: /* override */; --bs-primary-400: /* override */;
  --bs-primary-500: /* override */; --bs-primary-600: /* override */; --bs-primary-700: /* override */;
  --bs-primary-800: /* override */; --bs-primary-900: /* override */;

  /* Success */
  --bs-success-25: /* override */; --bs-success-50: /* override */; --bs-success-100: /* override */;
  --bs-success-200: /* override */; --bs-success-300: /* override */; --bs-success-400: /* override */;
  --bs-success-500: /* override */; --bs-success-600: /* override */; --bs-success-700: /* override */;
  --bs-success-800: /* override */; --bs-success-900: /* override */;

  /* Warning */
  --bs-warning-25: /* override */; --bs-warning-50: /* override */; --bs-warning-100: /* override */;
  --bs-warning-200: /* override */; --bs-warning-300: /* override */; --bs-warning-400: /* override */;
  --bs-warning-500: /* override */; --bs-warning-600: /* override */; --bs-warning-700: /* override */;
  --bs-warning-800: /* override */; --bs-warning-900: /* override */;

  /* Danger */
  --bs-danger-25: /* override */; --bs-danger-50: /* override */; --bs-danger-100: /* override */;
  --bs-danger-200: /* override */; --bs-danger-300: /* override */; --bs-danger-400: /* override */;
  --bs-danger-500: /* override */; --bs-danger-600: /* override */; --bs-danger-700: /* override */;
  --bs-danger-800: /* override */; --bs-danger-900: /* override */;

  /* Info */
  --bs-info-25: /* override */; --bs-info-50: /* override */; --bs-info-100: /* override */;
  --bs-info-200: /* override */; --bs-info-300: /* override */; --bs-info-400: /* override */;
  --bs-info-500: /* override */; --bs-info-600: /* override */; --bs-info-700: /* override */;
  --bs-info-800: /* override */; --bs-info-900: /* override */;

  /* Secondary */
  --bs-secondary-25: /* override */; --bs-secondary-50: /* override */; --bs-secondary-100: /* override */;
  --bs-secondary-200: /* override */; --bs-secondary-300: /* override */; --bs-secondary-400: /* override */;
  --bs-secondary-500: /* override */; --bs-secondary-600: /* override */; --bs-secondary-700: /* override */;
  --bs-secondary-800: /* override */; --bs-secondary-900: /* override */;
}
```

Dark mode (automatic and forced):
```css
@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
  :root {
    --bs-body-bg: #0e1116;
    --bs-body-color: #e6e6e6;
    --bs-heading-color: #ffffff;
    --bs-link-color: #5ba8ff;
    --bs-link-hover-color: #8fc2ff;
    --bs-border-color: #2a2f36;
  }
}
.dark {
  --bs-body-bg: #0e1116;
  --bs-body-color: #e6e6e6;
}
```

<br />

### Spacing scale
Override spacing globally or create theme scopes:
```css
:root {
  --bs-ref-spacer-4: 16px;  /* baseline */
  --bs-ref-spacer-6: 24px;
  --bs-ref-spacer-8: 32px;
  --bs-ref-spacer-12: 48px;
}
[data-bs-theme="compact"] {
  --bs-ref-spacer-6: 20px; /* tighter */
}
```

Refs (1–30)
Refs (1–30) is a reusable set of spacing reference tokens. Use these tokens as baseline measurements across components and layouts to avoid redefining values. Some tokens are used internally by Dynamic UI; you can override them to align with your design needs.
```css
:root {
  --bs-ref-spacer-1: 0.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-2: 0.5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-3: 0.75rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-4: 1rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-5: 1.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-6: 1.5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-7: 1.75rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-8: 2rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-9: 2.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-10: 2.5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-11: 2.75rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-12: 3rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-13: 3.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-14: 3.5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-15: 3.75rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-16: 4rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-17: 4.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-18: 4.5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-19: 4.75rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-20: 5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-21: 5.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-22: 5.5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-23: 5.75rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-24: 6rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-25: 6.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-26: 6.5rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-27: 6.75rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-28: 7rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-29: 7.25rem;
  --bs-ref-spacer-30: 7.5rem;
}
```

<br />

#### Borders, radius, shadows, focus
- Radius: `--bs-border-radius`, `--bs-border-radius-sm`, `--bs-border-radius-lg`, `--bs-border-radius-xl`, `--bs-border-radius-xxl`, `--bs-border-radius-pill`
- Border: `--bs-border-width`, `--bs-border-style`, `--bs-border-color`, `--bs-border-color-translucent`
- Shadows: `--bs-box-shadow`, `--bs-box-shadow-sm`, `--bs-box-shadow-lg`
- Focus ring: `--bs-focus-ring-width`, `--bs-focus-ring-opacity`, `--bs-focus-ring-border-color`, `--bs-focus-ring-color`

```css
:root {
  --bs-border-radius: .5rem;
  --bs-border-radius-lg: .75rem;
  --bs-box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,.08);
  --bs-focus-ring-width: 2px;
  --bs-focus-ring-opacity: .35;
  --bs-focus-ring-border-color: #0b74ff;
}
```

#### Border variables (full list)
```css
:root {
  --bs-border-width: /* override */;
  --bs-border-style: /* override */;
  --bs-border-color: /* override */;
  --bs-border-color-translucent: /* override */;

  --bs-border-radius: /* override */;
  --bs-border-radius-sm: /* override */;
  --bs-border-radius-lg: /* override */;
  --bs-border-radius-xl: /* override */;
  --bs-border-radius-xxl: /* override */;
  --bs-border-radius-2xl: /* alias of xxl */;
  --bs-border-radius-pill: /* override */;
}
```

<br />

## Component tokens (examples)
Many component styles are derived from the core variables, but some expose specific tokens:
- Buttons: variant tokens are generated off theme colors; customize via core color variables and (optionally) component CSS vars like --bs-btn-border-radius
- Alerts/Badges: read semantic tokens and bg-subtle/border-subtle
- Forms: validation colors map to --bs-form-valid-color/border-color, --bs-form-invalid-color/border-color

```css
/* Optional per-component tweak */
:root {
  --bs-btn-border-radius: var(--bs-border-radius-lg);
}
```

<br />

## Dark mode patterns
- Use dark: utilities for class-based overrides and @media prefers-color-scheme for system dark.
- Define token pairs for light/dark to ensure consistent tints and emphasis colors.

```css
.dark {
  --bs-secondary-bg: #1b2129;
  --bs-secondary-color: rgba(230,230,230,.75);
  --bs-danger-100: #471c1c; /* dark tint variant */
}
```

<br />

## Theming workflow (recommended)
1. Define brand color palette (primary/success/warning/danger/info/secondary + tints 25–900).
2. Set typography: body family/size, heading/display scales, small text, line-heights.
3. Tune spacing scale and component gaps using --bs-ref-spacer-*.
4. Adjust radius, borders, shadows, focus tokens for personality and accessibility.
5. Implement dark mode via prefers-color-scheme and .dark, validate contrast.
6. Verify utilities (fs-*, display-*, text-*, bg-*, border-*) reflect your overrides.

<br />

## Bootstrapping a theme (copy-paste starter)
```css
/* Global theme */
:root {
  /* Typography */
  --bs-body-font-family: "Jost", system-ui, sans-serif;
  --bs-body-font-size: 1rem;
  --bs-heading-line-height: 1.2;
  --bs-fs-small: .875rem;

  /* Color tokens */
  --bs-body-bg: #ffffff;
  --bs-body-color: #2e3438;
  --bs-primary: #0b74ff;
  --bs-success: #0c8a50;
  --bs-warning: #d99100;
  --bs-danger: #c83333;
  --bs-info: #0aa0c8;
  --bs-secondary: #5b6670;

  /* Spacing */
  --bs-ref-spacer-4: 16px;
  --bs-ref-spacer-6: 24px;

  /* Radius/Shadows */
  --bs-border-radius: .5rem;
  --bs-box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,.08);
}

/* System dark support */
@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
  :root {
    --bs-body-bg: #0e1116;
    --bs-body-color: #e6e6e6;
    --bs-border-color: #2a2f36;
  }
}
```

</div>

Design System/Foundations/Extended Utilities

design-system-foundations-extended-utilities--docs · ./stories/foundations/UtilitiesOverview.mdx
import { Meta } from '@storybook/addon-docs/blocks';

<Meta title="Design System/Foundations/Extended Utilities" />

<div className="inline-story sb-unstyled">

# Utilities Overview

Dynamic Framework extends Bootstrap utilities for speed and flexibility. Bootstrap’s core utilities are not all responsive by default; we provide responsive variants and extensions across display, alignment, spacing, typography, and more. Below are notable additions from our utilities layer.

<br />

### Variants: hover: and dark:
- Hover Utilities: <a href="/?path=/story/design-system-examples-hover-utilities">Design System/Examples/Hover Utilities</a>
- Dark Utilities: <a href="/?path=/story/design-system-examples-dark-utilities">Design System/Examples/Dark Utilities</a>

```html
<a class="text-body hover:text-danger">Danger on hover</a>
<div class="text-body dark:text-success">Success in dark</div>
```

<br />

### Spacing (0–30)
- Margin: `.m{t|b|s|e|x|y}-{0..30}`; Padding: `.p{t|b|s|e|x|y}-{0..30}` (responsive)

```html
<div class="mt-15 px-30 py-2">...</div>
```

<br />

### Extended display and alignment
- Display: `.d-{inline|inline-block|block|table|table-row|table-cell|flex|inline-flex|none|grid|table-header-group}` (responsive)
- Vertical align: `.v-align-{baseline|top|bottom|text-top|text-bottom|sub|super|middle}` (responsive)

```html
<div class="d-grid v-align-middle">...</div>
```

<br />

### Grid columns (CSS Grid)
- `.g-col-{13…24}` for larger grid spans (responsive)

```html
<div class="d-grid" style="grid-template-columns: repeat(24, 1fr)">
  <div class="g-col-6">6 cols</div>
  <div class="g-col-18">18 cols</div>
</div>
```

<br />

### Typography utilities
- Display font sizes: `.display-{1…6}` map to `--bs-fs-display-*` via `--bs-display-font-size`
- Body font size: `.fs-body`
- Line-height: `.lh-1`, `.lh-sm`, `.lh-base`, `.lh-lg`
- Text wrap: `.text-wrap-{balance|normal|truncate|wrap}`
- Text truncate (lines): `.text-truncate-{1…6}` (responsive)

```html
<div class="display-4">Display 4</div>
<p class="lh-base text-wrap-balance">Balanced wrapping</p>
<div class="text-truncate-3" style="max-width: 240px">Long text…</div>
```

See: <a href="/?path=/story/design-system-foundations-typography">Design System/Foundations/Typography</a>.

<br />

### Color utilities
- Text/background/border colors include palettes and grays: `.text-{token}`, `.bg-{token}-{25|50|100|200|300|400|500|600|700|800|900}`, `.border-{token}`
- Overlay opacity: `.overlay-{0|25|50|75|100}` (uses CSS var)
- Opacity and text-opacity: support `40` in addition to Bootstrap defaults

```html
<div class="bg-primary-100 overlay-50">Overlayed block</div>
```

<br />

### Size utilities
- Width/Height: `.w-*`, `.h-*` extended to be responsive
- Font-weight and position: responsive variants enabled

```html
<div class="position-relative h-100 w-100">...</div>
```

<br />

### Cursor utilities
- `.cursor-{auto|default|pointer|not-allowed|wait|text|crosshair|zoom-in|zoom-out|grab|grabbing}`

```html
<button class="cursor-pointer">Clickable</button>
```

<br />

### Animation utilities
- `.fade-in` — applies a quick opacity transition from `0` to `1` using `ease-in-out` (duration: `0.3s`).

```html
<div class="fade-in">This content fades in on render</div>
```

Useful for conditionally rendered elements, modals, alerts, or any content that appears dynamically. The animation runs once on mount and does not loop.

</div>

Design System/Foundations/Typography

design-system-foundations-typography--docs · ./stories/foundations/Typography.mdx
import { Meta } from '@storybook/addon-docs/blocks';

<Meta title="Design System/Foundations/Typography" />

<div className="inline-story sb-unstyled" style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--bs-body-font-family)' }}>

# Typography Foundations

Dynamic Framework standardizes typography on top of Bootstrap 5 using the Jost typeface, a clear size scale, semantic text colors, and helpful utilities for weight, line-height, wrapping, and truncation.

<br />

### Type scale and display styles

- Headings: h1–h6 and heading utility classes `.h1` … `.h6`
- Display styles: `.display-1` … `.display-6`
- Size utilities: `.fs-1` … `.fs-6`, `.small`
- Body size: `.fs-body`

<div className="d-flex flex-column gap-2 mt-2 mb-4">
  <div className="display-1">Display 1</div>
  <div className="display-4">Display 4</div>
  <h1>Heading H1</h1>
  <h3>Heading H3</h3>
  <p className="h1 m-0">Heading utility (.h1)</p>
  <p className="h4 m-0">Heading utility (.h4)</p>
  <p className="fs-4 m-0">Text with .fs-4</p>
  <p className="fs-body m-0">Body default (.fs-body)</p>
  <p className="small m-0 text-body-secondary">Small text (.small)</p>
</div>

```css
/* Display utilities map to CSS vars used by type rendering */
.display-1 { --bs-display-font-size: var(--bs-fs-display-1); }
.display-2 { --bs-display-font-size: var(--bs-fs-display-2); }
.display-3 { --bs-display-font-size: var(--bs-fs-display-3); }
.display-4 { --bs-display-font-size: var(--bs-fs-display-4); }
.display-5 { --bs-display-font-size: var(--bs-fs-display-5); }
.display-6 { --bs-display-font-size: var(--bs-fs-display-6); }
/* Base type consumes it: font-size: var(--bs-display-font-size) */

/* Size utilities */
.fs-1 { font-size: var(--bs-fs-1); }
.fs-2 { font-size: var(--bs-fs-2); }
.fs-3 { font-size: var(--bs-fs-3); }
.fs-4 { font-size: var(--bs-fs-4); }
.fs-5 { font-size: var(--bs-fs-5); }
.fs-6 { font-size: var(--bs-fs-6); }
.small { font-size: var(--bs-fs-small); }

/* Body size utility */
.fs-body    { font-size: var(--bs-body-font-size); }
```

<br />

### Semantic text colors

Use `.text-{token}` with semantic states and extended palettes:
- Tokens: Primary, Success, Warning, Danger, Info, Secondary, Light, Dark
- Shades: `{25|50|100|200|300|400|500|600|700|800|900}` for background tints: `.bg-{token}-{shade}`
- Light variants are intended for dark backgrounds

<div className="d-flex flex-wrap gap-3 mb-2 mb-4">
  <p className="m-0 text-primary">Primary text</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-success">Success text</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-warning">Warning text</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-danger">Danger text</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-info">Info text</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-secondary">Secondary text</p>
  <p className="m-0 text-dark">Dark text</p>
</div>

<div className="mt-2 p-2 rounded bg-dark text-light">Text-light over dark background</div>

<br />

### Font weight and line-height

- Font weight utilities (responsive enabled): `.fw-light`, `.fw-normal`, `.fw-semibold`, `.fw-bold`
- Line-height utilities: `.lh-1`, `.lh-sm`, `.lh-base`, `.lh-lg`

<div className="d-flex flex-column gap-2 mt-2 mb-4">
  <p className="fw-light my-1">Light weight</p>
  <p className="fw-normal my-1">Normal weight</p>
  <p className="fw-semibold my-1">Semibold weight</p>
  <p className="fw-bold my-1">Bold weight</p>
  <p className="lh-1 my-1">Line-height 1</p>
  <p className="lh-sm my-1">Line-height sm</p>
  <p className="lh-base my-1">Line-height base</p>
  <p className="lh-lg my-1">Line-height lg</p>
</div>

```css
/* Line-height utilities map to variables */
.lh-sm   { line-height: var(--bs-lh-sm); }
.lh-base { line-height: var(--bs-lh-base); }
.lh-lg   { line-height: var(--bs-lh-lg); }
```

<br />

### Text decoration and font style

- Underline: `.text-decoration-underline`
- Line-through: `.text-decoration-line-through`
- Italic: `.fst-italic`

<div className="d-flex flex-column gap-2 mt-2 mb-4">
  <p className="text-decoration-underline m-0">Underlined text</p>
  <p className="text-decoration-line-through m-0">Line-through text</p>
  <p className="fst-italic m-0">Italic text</p>
</div>

<br />

### Text wrapping and truncation

- Balanced wrapping: `.text-wrap-balance`
- Normal wrapping: `.text-wrap-normal`; Force wrap: `.text-wrap-wrap`
- Truncation by lines (responsive): `.text-truncate-{1..6}`

<div className="d-flex flex-column gap-2 mt-2 mb-4" style={{ maxWidth: 360 }}>
  <p className="text-wrap-balance">
    Balanced wrapping strives for visually even lines for better readability across varying widths.
  </p>
  <p className="text-wrap-wrap">
    Force wrapping when you need long identifiers or URLs to break across lines gracefully.
  </p>
  <p className="text-truncate-3">
    Long text that will be truncated to three lines. Long text that will be truncated to three lines. Long text that will be truncated to three lines. Long text that will be truncated to three lines with additional content to ensure overflow beyond three lines in typical widths. This sentence adds even more content so the ellipsis appears reliably across viewports. Yet another clause to extend the content further.
  </p>
</div>

```css
/* Text wrap utility values */
.text-wrap-balance { text-wrap: balance; }
.text-wrap-normal  { text-wrap: normal; }
.text-wrap-truncate{ text-wrap: truncate; }
.text-wrap-wrap    { text-wrap: wrap; }

/* Truncate uses CSS vars and -webkit-line-clamp under the hood */
```

<br />

### Dark mode and hover variants for text

- Dark mode variant: `.dark:text-{token}` adapts text color in dark contexts
- Hover variant: `.hover:text-{token}` provides interactive feedback on text

```html
<a class="text-body hover:text-danger">Hover to see danger color</a>
<div class="text-body dark:text-success">Text turns success in dark</div>
```

</div>
